The `migrateOverrides` function handles the overrides array separately from defaults. The comment indicates the author was aware that defaults.custom might not be present. Looking back at the problem: dashboards without explicit `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` are losing column widths and text alignment, which means the migration either needs to create this structure when missing or ensure existing data is properly preserved during the
